local script = Instance.new('LocalScript', Execute)

local execute = script.Parent
Editor = script.Parent.Parent.EditorScroller.Editor

execute.MouseButton1Click:Connect(
function()
assert(loadstring(Editor.Text))()
end
)

end

end

Tab:AddButton({
Name = "ğŸŒŒAimbotğŸŒŒ",
Callback = function()
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Holding = false

_G.AimbotEnabled = true
_G.TeamCheck = false -- If set to true then the script would only lock your aim at enemy team members.
_G.AimPart = "Head" -- Where the aimbot script would lock at.
_G.Sensitivity = 0 -- How many seconds it takes for the aimbot script to officially lock onto the target's aimpart.

_G.CircleSides = 64 -- How many sides the FOV circle would have.
_G.CircleColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) -- (RGB) Color that the FOV circle would appear as.
_G.CircleTransparency = 0.7 -- Transparency of the circle.
_G.CircleRadius = 80 -- The radius of the circle / FOV.
_G.CircleFilled = false -- Determines whether or not the circle is filled.
_G.CircleVisible = true -- Determines whether or not the circle is visible.
_G.CircleThickness = 0 -- The thickness of the circle.

local FOVCircle = Drawing.new("Circle")
FOVCircle.Position = Vector2.new(Camera.ViewportSize.X / 2, Camera.ViewportSize.Y / 2)
FOVCircle.Radius = _G.CircleRadius
FOVCircle.Filled = _G.CircleFilled
FOVCircle.Color = _G.CircleColor
FOVCircle.Visible = _G.CircleVisible
FOVCircle.Radius = _G.CircleRadius
FOVCircle.Transparency = _G.CircleTransparency
FOVCircle.NumSides = _G.CircleSides
FOVCircle.Thickness = _G.CircleThickness

local function GetClosestPlayer()
local MaximumDistance = _G.CircleRadius
local Target = nil

for _, v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
if v.Name ~= LocalPlayer.Name then
if _G.TeamCheck == true then
if v.Team ~= LocalPlayer.Team then
if v.Character ~= nil then
if v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") ~= nil then
if v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
local ScreenPoint = Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", math.huge).Position)
local VectorDistance = (Vector2.new(UserInputService:GetMouseLocation().X, UserInputService:GetMouseLocation().Y) - Vector2.new(ScreenPoint.X, ScreenPoint.Y)).Magnitude

if VectorDistance < MaximumDistance then
Target = v
end
end
end
end
end
else
if v.Character ~= nil then
if v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") ~= nil then
if v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
local ScreenPoint = Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", math.huge).Position)
local VectorDistance = (Vector2.new(UserInputService:GetMouseLocation().X, UserInputService:GetMouseLocation().Y) - Vector2.new(ScreenPoint.X, ScreenPoint.Y)).Magnitude

if VectorDistance < MaximumDistance then
Target = v
end
end
end
end
end
end
end

return Target
end

Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  Holding = false
Â Â Â  end
end)

Â Â Â  FOVCircle.Filled = _G.CircleFilled
Â Â Â  FOVCircle.Color = _G.CircleColor
Â Â Â  FOVCircle.Visible = _G.CircleVisible

Â Â Â  FOVCircle.NumSides = _G.CircleSides
Â Â Â  FOVCircle.Thickness = _G.CircleThickness

Â Â Â  if Holding == true and _G.AimbotEnabled == true then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  TweenService:Create(Camera, TweenInfo.new(_G.Sensitivity, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {CFrame = CFrame.new(Camera.CFrame.Position, GetClosestPlayer().Character[_G.AimPart].Position)}):Play()
Â Â Â  end
end)

Â  endÂ Â Â

local orgp = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position

local function teleport()
while istping do
local randomPosition = orgp + Vector3.new(math.random(-15, 15), math.random(-15, 35), math.random(-15, 15))
player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(randomPosition)
wait()
end
end

if key == thekeybindis then
if istping then
istping = false
player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(orgp)
else 
istping = true
orgp = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
teleport()
end
end
end)

function getClosestPlayerToCursor(trg_part)
Â Â Â  local nearest = nil
Â Â Â  local last = math.huge
Â Â Â  for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  if v ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v.Team ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Team and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and v.Character and v.Character:FindFirstChild(trg_part) then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(trg_part) then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local ePos, vissss = workspace.CurrentCamera:WorldToViewportPoint(v.Character[trg_part].Position)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local AccPos = Vector2.new(ePos.x, ePos.y)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local mousePos = Vector2.new(workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.x / 2, workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.y / 2)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local distance = (AccPos - mousePos).magnitude
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  if distance < last and vissss and distance < 400 then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  last = distance
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  nearest = v
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  end
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  end
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  end
Â Â Â  end
Â Â Â  return nearest
end

Â  endÂ Â Â

Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(255, 165, 0), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(0, 128, 0), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 255), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(75, 0, 130), 
Â Â Â  Color3.fromRGB(238, 130, 238)
}

local head = character:WaitForChild("Head")

fpsLabel.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)

local fpsTextLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
fpsTextLabel.Parent = fpsLabel
fpsTextLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
fpsTextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
fpsTextLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
fpsTextLabel.TextScaled = true

local function formatFPS(fps)
Â Â Â  return string.format("ğŸŒŒ-J-ğŸŒŒ", math.floor(fps + 0.5))
end

local lastFrameTime = tick()
local frameCount = 0

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
Â Â Â  local currentTime = tick()
Â Â Â  frameCount += 1
Â Â Â  if currentTime - lastFrameTime >= 1 then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  local fps = frameCount / (currentTime - lastFrameTime)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  fpsTextLabel.Text = formatFPS(fps)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  frameCount = 0
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  lastFrameTime = currentTime
Â Â Â  end
end)

UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(inputObject)
Â Â Â  if inputObject.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  fpsLabel.Enabled = not fpsLabel.Enabled
Â Â Â  end
end)

StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.All, false)

while true do
Â Â Â  fpsTextLabel.TextColor3 = colors[colorIndex]
Â Â Â  colorIndex = colorIndex % #colors + 1
Â Â Â  wait(0.10)
end
Â Â Â Â Â  print("button pressed")
Â  endÂ Â Â  
})
